| <span data-ttu-id="f3cb6-449">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f3cb6-449">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f3cb6-450">Valor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f3cb6-450">Value</span></span> |
